<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">be-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lust.html>lust</a></i>. <span class="maintenance-line"><i>This etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> incomplete. </p>

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:belust.html>belust</a></strong> (<i>not comparable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>eager, desiring [+ <span><i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a></i> <span>(for, to)</span></span>] <span class="defdate">[from 16th c.]</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:onverbiddelijk.html>Onverbiddelijk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:genadeloos.html>genadeloos</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:stapten.html>stapten</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:eenden.html>eenden</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nader.html>nader</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:zeer.html>zeer</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:belust.html>belust</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:brood.html>brood</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Unrelenting and mercilessly the ducks stepped <a href = vnd.unilang:closer.html>closer</a>, deeply <b>craving for</b> bread.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<ul><li>Instead of <i><a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:om.html>om</a></i> can be used when the argument <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> an infinitive.</li>
<li>In older texts the prepositions <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tot.html>tot</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:naar.html>naar</a></i> or a complement genitive may be used in the same meaning as the preposition <i><a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a></i> that <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> used in modern language. These old usages are now obsolete.</li></ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bemachtigen.html>bemachtigen</a> (10520)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:bemachtigen.html>bemachtigen</a></i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">be-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:macht.html>macht</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-igen</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bemachtigen.html>bemachtigen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to acquire with difficulty</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to subdue, to overpower</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to empower, to give power to</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Werkwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:werkwoord.html>Werkwoord</a></i></span></h4>

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bemoeien.html>bemoeien</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:al.html>al</a></i>, literally ‚Äúmeddle-all‚Äù.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bemoeial.html>bemoeial</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> or <abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bemoeiallen.html>bemoeiallen</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bemoeials.html>bemoeials</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bemoeial.html>bemoeialletje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A busybody, a meddlesome person.</li></ol>

<ol><li>intervention, meddling <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">usually with a negative connotation</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>

***bende.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bende.html>bende</a> (1923)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:bende.html>bende</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro"><a href = vnd.unilang:bende.html>bende</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Frankish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Frankish language">Frankish</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*bend</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*bandiz</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*b ∞end ∞-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">‚Äú</span><span class="mention-gloss">to tie; bond, <a href = vnd.unilang:band.html>band</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">‚Äù</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:band.html>band</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bende.html>bende</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bendes.html>bendes</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:benden.html>benden</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bende.html>bendetje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:gang.html>gang</a>, squad</li>
<li>mess as in: a disagreeable mixture of a large quantity of <a href = vnd.unilang:objects.html>objects</a> in disorder resulting from people misbehaving or animals stampeding.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bent.html>bent</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gij.html>gij</a></i>, by analogy of other <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-de</i> verb contractions. The personal agreement <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> ungrammatical in standard Dutch, and <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> based on contamination with <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ben.html>ben</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:jij.html>jij</a></i>.
</p>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<p>The contraction <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> sometimes reinforced with an additional <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gij.html>gij</a></i>, giving <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bende.html>bende</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gij.html>gij</a></i>.
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bender.html>bender</a> (16573)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Latn mention" lang="en">bend</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:dictatoriaal.html>-er</a></i>. In sense of ‚Äúheavy drinking‚Äù, originally generally ‚Äúspree‚Äù, from 1846,<sup id="cite_ref-oetyld_1-0" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-oetyld-1"> | 1 | </a></sup> of uncertain origin ‚Äì vague contemporary sense of ‚Äúsomething extraordinary‚Äù, connection to <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">bend</i> (e.g., bending elbow to <a href = vnd.unilang:drink.html>drink</a>) or perhaps from Scottish sense of ‚Äústrong drinker‚Äù.<sup id="cite_ref-oetyld_1-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-oetyld-1"> | 1 | </a></sup>
</p>

</p>
<ol><li>One who, or that which, bends.</li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:beneden.html>beneden</a> (499)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:beneden.html>beneden</a></i>. <span class="maintenance-line"><i>This etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> incomplete. <hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

</p>

***benemen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:benemen.html>benemen</a> (71002)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">benƒìmen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*bineman</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*binemanƒÖ</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">be-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:nemen.html>nemen</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:benemen.html>benemen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to take away; snatch</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to purloin, to rob, to steal, to filch, to swipe</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Werkwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:werkwoord.html>Werkwoord</a></i></span></h4>

***benoemen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:benoemen.html>benoemen</a> (12951)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:benoemen.html>benoemen</a></i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">be-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:noemen.html>noemen</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:benoemen.html>benoemen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to appoint, to nominate
